### Round 9: German Grand Prix
*Date: 1990-07-29*

#### Qualifying Results

| Driver | Constructor | Grid | Starting ELO | Change | New ELO | vs Teammate |

### Round 12: Italian Grand Prix
*Date: 1990-09-09*

#### Qualifying Results

| Driver | Constructor | Grid | Starting ELO | Change | New ELO | vs Teammate |
